beginState: s32'BitNDie_EVENT'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
    homingClear: 
    linkObjPosition: 0
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
      ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
      stopLinkObject: 0
    endIf: 
    landingHeight: 0
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
      upon: (WALL_BREAK)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'box'
        onSpriteChange: s32'ram060_weapon_R_00'
        addPositionX: 0, -150000
        addPositionY: 0, 350000
        upon: (FRAME_STEP)
          if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
            callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_LH_Self'
            ignoreFinishStop: 1
            ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
            stopLinkObject: 0
          endIf: 
        endUpon: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_LH_Self'
    endElse: 
    spriteSlowParam: 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
    spriteSlowParamFinishStop: 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
  endUpon: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'box', Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_00', 1
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_01', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_02', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_03', 3
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_04', 3
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_05', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_06', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_07', 1
  endLabel: 
  sendValuesToObject: 0, 1, 0, 0
  createObjectWithArg: s32'404wepR_summon_short', (PLAYER)
  setAlphaColor: 0
  sprite: s32'null', 3
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'box'
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_00', 4
  setAlphaColor: 255
  haltMomentum: 1
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 10000
  setGravity: 1000
  upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
    gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_01', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_02', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_03', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_04', 4
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'loop'
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_05', 5
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_06', 5
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'
  beginLabel: s32'landing'
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_07', 5
  haltMomentum: 1
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_08', 5
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_09', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_10', 3
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_11', 3

endState:

          ignoreFinishStop: 1

beginSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
  ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
      jumpToState: s32'BitNCrouch'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      jumpToState: s32'BitFCrouch'
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
      jumpToState: s32'BitN'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      jumpToState: s32'BitF'
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'ram_BitAction'
  ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
      jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNDie'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFDie'
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(ObjReg1)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
    checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActEntryWait'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
      displayModel: 0
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(ObjReg3)
      storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Tmp), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
      ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Mem(Dir)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNTurn'
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNCrouchTurn'
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNAirTurn'
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFTurn'
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFCrouchTurn'
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFAirTurn'
          endIf: 
        endElse:

beginSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnCutScene_ObjHide'
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
  landingHeight: -268435455
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
    linkPawnWithAnimation: s32'Weapon_R', s32''
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    linkPawnWithAnimation: s32'Weapon_L', s32''
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
  endElse: 
  linkObjectZ: 3
  stopLinkObject: 3
  linkObjPosition: 0
  linkObjectAngle: 0
  setDepth: 0
  homing: (DISTANCE_ACCELERATION), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 0, 30
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
    ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
      ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamage)
        ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
          homing: (DISTANCE_ACCELERATION), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 60, 0, 0
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(AngleY), (PLAYER), Mem(AngleY)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  upon: (IDLING)
    callSubroutine: s32'ram_BitAction'
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(PosZ), (PLAYER), Mem(PosZ)
  endUpon: 
  upon: (WALL_BREAK)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
      ifNotInObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_EXIT)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (TOUCH_GROUND)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
        linkObjPosition: 3
        linkObjectAngle: 3
        ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
          homingClear: 
          linkObjPosition: 0
          ignoreFinishStop: 1
          ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
          stopLinkObject: 0
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNDie'
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFDie'
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifTrueInObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
            pauseSprite: 1
            upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
              pauseSprite: 0
              clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_EXIT)
              linkObjPosition: 0
              linkObjectAngle: 0
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
                jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNWSB'
              endIf: 
              else: 
                jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFWSB'
              endElse: 
            endUpon: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitN'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitF'
            endElse: 
          endElse: 
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
    ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
    stopLinkObject: 0
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
      jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitNDamage'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'BitFDamage'
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (FRAME_STEP)
    checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'BitNLaser'
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'BitFLaser'
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'BajonetoC'
        ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
          checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'BajonetoD'
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            if: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
              storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(PosZ), (PLAYER), Mem(PosZ)
              setNoCollision: 1
              ifOperationInObject: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
                pushboxHeightLow: 0
                ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance)
                  setPushboxWidth: 110000
                  setPushboxHeight: 300000
                endIf: 
                else: 
                  setPushboxWidth: 120000
                  setPushboxHeight: 250000
                endElse: 
              endIf: 
              else: 
                setPushboxWidth: 100000
                setPushboxHeight: 275000
                pushboxHeightLow: -125000
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
            else: 
              setNoCollision: 0
            endElse: 
            ifNot: Mem(BattleDoing)
              setNoCollision: 0
            endIf: 
            ifTrueInObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg19)
              linkObjPosition: 3
            endIf: 
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActLockWait'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              linkObjPosition: 3
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'BitNDie'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
    homingClear: 
    linkObjPosition: 0
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
      ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
      stopLinkObject: 0
    endIf: 
    landingHeight: 0
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
      upon: (WALL_BREAK)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'box'
        onSpriteChange: s32'ram060_weapon_R_00'
        addPositionX: 0, -150000
        addPositionY: 0, 350000
        upon: (FRAME_STEP)
          if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
            callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_LH_Self'
            ignoreFinishStop: 1
            ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
            stopLinkObject: 0
          endIf: 
        endUpon: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_LH_Self'
    endElse: 
    spriteSlowParam: 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
    spriteSlowParamFinishStop: 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0
  endUpon: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'box', Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_00', 1
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_01', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_02', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_03', 3
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_04', 3
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_05', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_06', 2
  sprite: s32'ram050_weapon_R_07', 1
  endLabel: 
  sendValuesToObject: 0, 1, 0, 0
  createObjectWithArg: s32'404wepR_summon_short', (PLAYER)
  setAlphaColor: 0
  sprite: s32'null', 3
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'box'
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_00', 4
  setAlphaColor: 255
  haltMomentum: 1
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 10000
  setGravity: 1000
  upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
    gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_01', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_02', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_03', 4
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_04', 4

  haltMomentum: 1
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_08', 5
  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_09', 4

  sprite: s32'ram060_weapon_R_11', 3

beginState: s32'BitNBurst'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
    upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
      callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
    endUpon: 
    upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(SpeedY), Val(0)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'Bakuhatsu'
        upon: (FALL_SPEED)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (FALL_SPEED)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Drop'
          upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
            ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
              jumpToState: s32'BitNLanding'
            endIf: 
          endUpon: 
        endUpon: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_00', 2
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_01', 2
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'Bakuhatsu'
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_02', 3
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_03', 3
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'loop'
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_04', 3
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_05', 3
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'
  beginLabel: s32'Drop'
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_06', 3
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_07', 3
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'downloop'
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_08', 3
  sprite: s32'ram330_weapon_R_09', 3
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'downloop'
endState: 

beginState: s32'BitNWSB'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(PosZ), (PLAYER), Mem(PosZ)
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
    endIf: 
    homingClear: 
    displayModel: 0
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamage)
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 15
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 1
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    endElse: 
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
            if: Mem(ActReg0)
              addPositionX: 0, -5000000
              addPositionY: 0, 500000
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
        endIf: 
        if: Mem(ActReg1)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'BitNLaser'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
        displayMesh: s32'Wep_Open_R', 1
        displayMesh: s32'Weapon_R', 0
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'BitNMorutobato'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      displayMesh: s32'Wep_Open_R', 1
      displayMesh: s32'Weapon_R', 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'Neutral'
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'

beginState: s32'BitNWSB_Bajoneto'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(PosZ), (PLAYER), Mem(PosZ)
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(AngleY), (PLAYER), Mem(AngleY)
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
    endIf: 
    homingClear: 
    haltMomentum: 1
    displayModel: 0
    setAlphaColor: 0
    setAngle: -40000
    sendValuesToObject: 0, 1, 0, 1
    createObjectWithArg: s32'wep_ShotRecovery_S', (PLAYER)
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamage)
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 15
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 1
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    endElse: 
    ifNotInObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 2
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      displayModel: 1
      setAlphaColor: 255
      callSubroutine: s32'cmnWSB_Event_Status'
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ReturnValue), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ReturnValue), Val(2)
          callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
            if: Mem(ActReg0)
              addPositionX: 0, -5000000
              addPositionY: 0, 500000
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
        endIf: 
        if: Mem(ActReg1)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
          if: Mem(ActReg2)
            displayModel: 0
            setAlphaColor: 0
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'Neutral'
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
endState:

beginState: s32'BitFWSB'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(PosZ), (PLAYER), Mem(PosZ)
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
      ignoreFinishStop: 1
    endIf: 
    homingClear: 
    displayModel: 0
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamage)
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 15
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 1
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    endElse: 
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
            if: Mem(ActReg0)
              addPositionX: 0, -5000000
              addPositionY: 0, 500000
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
        endIf: 
        if: Mem(ActReg1)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'BitFLaser'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
        displayMesh: s32'Wep_Open_L', 1
        displayMesh: s32'Weapon_L', 0
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'BitFMorutobato'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      displayMesh: s32'Wep_Open_L', 1
      displayMesh: s32'Weapon_L', 0
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'Neutral'
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
endState:

      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 15
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf:

      setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 1
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)

        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ReturnValue), Val(2)
          callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)

            if: Mem(ActReg0)
              addPositionX: 0, -5000000
              addPositionY: 0, 500000

          moveToObject: (PLAYER)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'Neutral'
          if: Mem(ActReg2)
            displayModel: 0
            setAlphaColor: 0
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon:

beginState: s32'BitF6P'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'BitReset'
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(0)
    checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActAirBDash'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      haltMomentum: 1
      homingClear: 
      moveToObject: (PLAYER)
      linkObjPosition: 3
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(12)
          addPositionY: 0, 2500
        endIf: 
        else: 
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
            callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
          endUpon: 
        endElse: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActRomanCancel'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        if: Mem(ActReg1)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
      upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
        storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
        callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'
      endUpon: 
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'ram210_weapon_L_01', 2
  sprite: s32'ram210_weapon_L_02', 2
  sprite: s32'ram210_weapon_L_03', 3

    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)

    haltMomentum: 1
    storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
    upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
      callSubroutine: s32'BitActionNeutral'

      checkLastStateName: s32'Bit_NoDisp'
